Settings languages here will filter the streams in 'Top Channels' and game-specific streams by language\r\n- Can now view channel-specific emoticons in a separate pivot than all Twitch emoticons (now separated into Global and Channel)\r\n- Channel (profile) videos now show highlights, archive and uploaded videos\r\n- Moved to a native way of displaying emotes and gifs. As a result they now load faster and don't impact performance as much\r\n- Reduced frequency (by half) of prompt to rate & review dialog\r\n- Removed Donate button from menu (wasn't getting any donations anyway -- might be about time I open source Unstream...)\r\n- Fixed issue where characters from other languages were unreadable (e.g. cyrillic)\r\n- Fixed issue where refresh was not working (e.g. refreshing followed channels)\"\r\n- Fixed issue where lists would sometimes show duplicates (e.g duplicate stream items, channel feed)\r\n- Fixed issue where copying user nickname from chat (users pivot) would not work\r\n- Fixed issue where chat replay for VODs would (sometimes) not load after switching VODs\"\r\n- Fixed issue where refresh on full-screen chat would not work\r\n\r\nv4.1.1.0 - 02/10/2016\r\n- Added push notifications for alerts so I can let you guys know when there's an issue (no support for push notifications for when streams go live yet sorry!)\r\n- Fixed connectivity issues for Continue App Experience (handover feature) -- now more reliable\r\n- Fixed notification mirroring and universal dismiss for generic toast (X streamers live)\r\n- Unstream now requires W10 AU update - due to all the new features that only AU devices can support :)\r\n\r\nv4.1.0.0 - 29/09/2016\r\n- Continue App Experience is here! You can now handover from a stream/VOD (note that VOD seek position is retained!) to another device (directly to stream/VOD or chat). Option can be found in the '...' in stream/VOD view\r\n- Added notification mirroring and universal dimsiss! Notifications are now mirrored across devices (if app is not installed on other devices), or if app is installed on multiple devices, when you dismiss a notification on a single device, it will dismiss across all devices.\r\n- Optimised chat scrolling. Should now be way more performant (thansk to W10 AU update!)\r\n- VODs now retain seek position when switching quality\r\n- GIFs will now only repeat 5 times to prevent app slow downs and high CPU usage\r\n- Updated code which launches feedback hub\r\n- Fixed issue where stream/VOD would pause when locking the device\r\n- Fixed issue where back button would not appear when navigating directly to a stream (via notification or pinned tile)\r\n- Fixed issue where back button would work incorrectly when mini player is disabled\r\n- Fixed issue where notifications when streamers go live was not working after updating to W10 AU\r\n- Fixed issue where sending a message in chat would cause an error\r\n\r\nv4.0.3.0 - 17/09/2016\r\n- Fixed issue where stream list would not load on some pages\r\n\r\nv4.0.2.0 - 15/09/2016\r\n- Added options for stream delay (change this if you experience streams pausing while audio continues -- it is because stream has caught up to live content)\r\n- Fixed issue where login settings would reset often\r\n- Fixed issue where streams and videos would not load\r\n\r\nv4.0.1.0 - 26/07/2016\r\n- Fixed issue with content not loading\r\n\r\nv4.0.0.0 - 25/07/2016\r\n- Unstream is now completely free of ads!\r\n- Chat Replay is here!! View channel feed posts via new pivot item in profile page (view post and reactions only at the moment -- posting reactions and comments coming soon)\r\n- Added option to enable or disable mini player mode\r\n- (Re)Added ability to follow / unfollow games\r\n- Added notification aggregation. If there are more than 5 followed streams live, you will only be notified that there are 'multiple streamers live' and not one notification for each (some people have many followed streamers and would therefore be spammed)\r\n- Added donation options to About page\r\n- Increased number of seek steps (default 100) for VODs longer than 1 hour (to 1000 steps) and > 10 hours (to 10000 steps). Should now be able to seek more accurately!\r\n- Updated stream offset to reduce delays. Stream should now be closer to 'live' (previously a slight delay of 10 to 30 seconds)\r\n- Updated recent streams to use stream banner instead of live banner\r\n- Streams and VODs now exit fullscreen mode when finished\r\n- Minor UI updates\r\n- Fixed issue where VODs that required a subscription to watch were not loading, even if you were subscribed\r\n- Fixed issue with accents not displaying correctly (e.g. PokÃ©mon Go).
